#Vivekanand L. Swami 1st July, 2016

CREATE TABLE `defaultcustomfields` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `countryid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `stateid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `maxlength` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `fieldtype` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `fieldlabel` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `moduleid` smallint(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `customfield` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `customcolumn` tinyint(3) unsigned NOT NULL,
   KEY `countryid` (`countryid`),
   KEY `stateid` (`stateid`),
   CONSTRAINT `defaultcustomfields_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`countryid`) REFERENCES `country` (`id`),
   CONSTRAINT `defaultcustomfields_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`stateid`) REFERENCES `state` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#Raveesh Pathak 8th July 2016
CREATE TABLE consolidationdata (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `stakeinpercentage` double DEFAULT 0,
  `childcompany` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `consolidationdata_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`childcompany`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `consolidationdata_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE consolidationexchangeratedetails (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `applydate` DATE DEFAULT NULL,
  `exchangerate` double DEFAULT 0,
  `consolidationdata` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `consolidationexchangeratedetails_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`consolidationdata`) REFERENCES `consolidationdata` (`id`)
)
ENGINE=InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARACTER SET=utf8;

# Suhas Chaware 11 July 2016

CREATE TABLE `forecasttemplate` (
`id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`title` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`forecastid` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`forecasttype` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
`forecastmethod` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`forecastyear` date NOT NULL, 
`forecastyearhistory` varchar(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
`createdon` date NOT NULL, 
`modifiedon` date NOT NULL, 
`company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,  
`createdby` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
`modifiedby` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL, 
PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
FOREIGN KEY (`createdby`)  REFERENCES `users`(`userid`),
FOREIGN KEY (`modifiedby`)  REFERENCES `users`(`userid`))ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `forecastproductmapping` (
`id`  varchar(255) NOT NULL ,
`forecasttemplate`  varchar(255) NULL DEFAULT NULL ,
`product`  varchar(255) NULL DEFAULT NULL,
`company`  varchar(255) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`forecasttemplate`) REFERENCES `forecasttemplate` (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`))
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET=utf8;

#Pandurang 12th July 2016
alter table purchaseorder 
add column `dateofdelivery` date Default NULL,
add column `dateofshipment` date Default NULL,
add column `excisedutychargees` double DEFAULT '0',
add column `jobworklocation` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
add column `shipmentroute` varchar(255) DEFAULT '',
add column `gatepass` varchar(255) DEFAULT '',
add column `otherremarks` varchar(255) DEFAULT '',
add column  `workorderid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
add column  `product` varchar(255) Default NULL,
add column `productquantity` double DEFAULT '0',
add FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
add FOREIGN KEY (`jobworklocation`) REFERENCES `inventorylocation` (`id`);

alter table purchaseorder 
add column `ismrpjobworkout` char(1) DEFAULT 'F';

alter table goodsreceipt 
add column `ismrpjobworkin` char(1) DEFAULT 'F';

CREATE TABLE `customcurrency` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `currencyid` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `name` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `systemcurrencysymbol` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `systemcurrencycode` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `customcurrencysymbol` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `customcurrencycode` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `companyid` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
   CONSTRAINT `customcurrency_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`currencyid`) REFERENCES `currency` (`currencyid`),
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#Ajit Ankalle 28th July 2016
CREATE TABLE `taxexchangerate` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `tocurrency` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `fromcurrency` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `FJ554511836C21DA1A` (`fromcurrency`),
  KEY `FJ55451183DCC94449` (`tocurrency`),
  CONSTRAINT `FJ554511836C21DA1A` FOREIGN KEY (`tocurrency`) REFERENCES `currency` (`currencyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FJ55451183DCC94449` FOREIGN KEY (`fromcurrency`) REFERENCES `currency` (`currencyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `taxexchangeratedetails` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `applydate` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `exchangerate` double NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `exchangeratelink` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `todate` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `exchangeorder` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `foreigntobaseexchangerate` double NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `exchangeorder` (`exchangeorder`),
  KEY `FJ9C28B75F7E350557` (`company`),
  KEY `FJ9C28B75F1AE5B04F` (`exchangeratelink`),
  CONSTRAINT `FJ9C28B75F1AE5B04F` FOREIGN KEY (`exchangeratelink`) REFERENCES `taxexchangerate` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FJ9C28B75F7E350557` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO `taxexchangerate` SELECT * FROM `exchangerate`;
INSERT INTO `taxexchangeratedetails` SELECT * FROM `exchangeratedetails`;
